 1334 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     77 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0428               | * Register 1 - Volume and tone controls
 1335 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     78 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0428               | * Register 1 sets the volume and tone controls and is three bytes in length.
 1336 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     79 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0428               | * Talk 1 has a fourth byte appended which is the firmware revision of the FM Radio (mine is 0x0A).

 1339 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     82 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0428               | * 23-16  Volume, apparently set in increments of 0x11 by the application
 1340 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     83 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0428               | *    15  Always zero
 1341 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     84 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0428               | * 14-12  Treble
 1342 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     85 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0428               | *    11  Always zero
 1343 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     86 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0428               | *  10-8  Bass
 1344 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     87 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0428               | *     7  Mute, active high
 1345 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     88 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0428               | *   6-5  Sound fading, 0 = normal, 1 = low, 2 = medium, 3 = high
 1346 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     89 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0428               | *   4-1  Undetermined, apparently always zero
 1347 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     90 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0428               | *     0  Undetermined, initially zero but always set high by the application
